<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Interim Management Report</font></b></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">1. Business Activity</font></b></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
(&#147;the AIXTRON Group&#148; or &#147;the Company&#148;) is a leading provider of deposition
equipment to the semiconductor industry. The Company&#146;s technology solutions are
used by a diverse range of customers worldwide to build advanced components for
electronic and opto-electronic applications based on compound, silicon, or
organic semiconductor materials. Such components are used in displays,
signaling, lighting, fiber optic communication systems, wireless and mobile
telephony applications, optical and electronic storage devices, computing, as
well as a range of other leading-edge technologies.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company markets and sells its products worldwide, principally through its
direct sales organization and appointed dealers and sales representatives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s
business activities include developing, producing and installing equipment for
coating semiconductor materials, process engineering, consulting and training,
including ongoing customer support.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
supplies to customers both full production-scale complex material deposition systems
and small scale systems for Research and Development (R&amp;D) use and
small-scale production use.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s
product range includes customized production and research scale compound
semiconductor systems capable of depositing material films on up to 95 two-inch
diameter wafers per single production run, or smaller multiples of 4 to 6 inch
diameter wafers, employing Metal-Organic Chemical Vapor Deposition (MOCVD) or
Hydride Vapor Phase Epitaxy (HVPE) or organic thin film deposition on up to
Gen. 3.5 substrates, including Polymer Vapor Phase Deposition (PVPD) or Organic
Vapor Phase Deposition (OVPD</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">) or large area deposition for
Organic Light Emitting Diodes (OLED) applications or Plasma Enhanced Chemical
Vapor Phase Deposition (PECVD) for depositing complex Carbon Nanostructures
(Carbon Nanotubes or Nanowires).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
also manufactures full production and research scale deposition systems for
silicon semiconductor applications capable of depositing material films on
wafers of up to 300 mm diameter, employing technologies such as: Chemical Vapor
Deposition (CVD), Atomic Vapor Deposition (AVD</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">) and Atomic Layer Deposition
(ALD).</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3<a name="PB_3_150948_2897"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">2. Important Factors of the Reporting Period</font></b></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">US Dollar
development</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first
quarter of the year, the US Dollar strengthened against the Euro, which itself
remained under pressure with increasing tensions and uncertainties about
financial aid for Greece and the fiscal health of other peripheral Euro zone
countries. In February, the US Dollar also received fiscal support, when the
Federal Reserve, rather unexpectedly, raised the discount rate by 25bp.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The US Dollar
started the year 2010 with an exchange rate of USD 1.43 against the Euro, but
by the end of the first quarter, was approximately 6% stronger at 1.35 USD/EUR.
The quarterly average price was 1.40 USD/EUR (Q4/2009: 1.48 USD/EUR; Q1/2009:
1.30 USD/EUR) and the strengthening of the US Dollar during the quarter had a
positive influence on AIXTRON&#146;s Q1/2010 revenues and profitability.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Another
quarter of revenue growth with further increasing profitability</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Due to increasing
volume demand and influenced by the stronger US Dollar, revenues increased by
31% to EUR 154.5m over the last quarter, leading to a 3 percentage points
higher gross margin of 50% in Q1/2010. At the same time, the operating result
increased by 38% to EUR 46.4m with a one percentage point higher EBIT margin of
30%. Q1/2010 was the fourth sequential quarter of rising revenues and the third
sequential quarter of rising EBIT performance.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Market
introduction of AIXTRON&#146;s new generation products</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In February&nbsp;2010,
we announced the launch of AIXTRON&#146;s next generation MOCVD systems, the AIX G5
HT and CRIUS</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;II, which can be installed into
the new IC 2 platform, which was released at the same time. The market response
to these new generation products has been very encouraging, with several
multiple purchase orders already being received. Some systems have already been
delivered and acceptance signed by significant leading customers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based on the
proven Planetary and Showerhead Reactor designs, the AIX G5 HT and the CRIUS</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;II systems feature the largest wafer capacity
available on the market. Additional features include: a 20% smaller footprint,
higher growth rates and process pressures, as well as automation options.
Coupled with the elimination of the baking process, our new systems enable
cutting-edge levels of productivity, material quality and cost-of-ownership for
our customers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We believe that the
capabilities of these new tools, once again take us one step ahead of the
competition, underpinning our claim for technology and market leadership.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AIXTRON
2009 MOCVD market share confirmed at 68%</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based on
information published by Gartner Dataquest, an independent semiconductor
industry research company, in March&nbsp;2010, the AIXTRON MOCVD market share
has been confirmed at 68% in a total equipment market valued at USD 533m for
2009. </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This market share is in line with our previously
expressed</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Management
expectations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AIXTRON
expands to new R&amp;D facilities</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In January&nbsp;2010,
we announced our plans to build a new, state-of-the-art R&amp;D center to
support our Company&#146;s accelerated Research&nbsp;&amp; Development strategy and
increased focus on new product development.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
ground-breaking ceremony for the new facility was held on April&nbsp;14 and it
is planned that the first engineers will occupy their new offices by Q4/2010.
The new facility will be able to host up to 350 engineers, significantly
increasing the resources available to develop next generation complex material
deposition systems.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the very
positive compound semiconductor market environment, where the number of market
players is increasing, and product cycle times are decreasing, we believe that
focused and market-led R&amp;D is a critical success factor, in order to remain
the recognized technology and market leader in a period of projected growth.
Therefore, we are specifically increasing our R&amp;D focus on the
opportunities that could arise from the potentially faster than expected
arrival of a volume market for solid state lighting devices.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We are also currently actively
engaged in several research projects, including &#151; but not exclusively</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4<a name="PB_4_150948_3020"></a></font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;
projects aiming at novel nano-material concepts based on nanowire and nanotube
structures and extended developments of the Company&#146;s OVPD</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">/large area
deposition process technology, on which emerging small-molecule OLED special
lighting and signage applications can be produced and qualified.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Chinese
government sponsorships and initiatives</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Towards the end
of 2009, we experienced increasing demand from Chinese and Taiwanese companies
benefiting from Chinese central and local government subsidies. These Chinese
subsidies, which have now been extended into the current year, consist of
substantial cash incentives for investments in MOCVD production equipment and
reflect the strong strategic motivation of the Chinese government to invest in,
and to encourage, the Chinese LED industry.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Separately, the
Taiwanese government had &#151; until the end of 2009 &#151; offered tax incentives for
specific capital equipment investments, including the purchase of MOCVD
equipment. It is not yet known if this will be repeated in 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Some orders,
given under these incentive programs, have been booked during Q1/2010, and
further such bookings are expected during the next few quarters. However, in
line with our prudent order recognition policy, orders and backlog will only be
recorded, when all our internal profitability and sustainability requirements
are fulfilled.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Planned
conversion into European Company (SE)</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Executive
Board and Supervisory Board of AIXTRON AG have proposed converting the Company&#146;s
legal form from a German AG (Aktiengesellschaft) into a European SE (Societas
Europaea) and to adopt the name AIXTRON SE. The AIXTRON shareholders will be
asked to resolve upon the contemplated conversion of the legal form in the
General Meeting on May&nbsp;18, 2010. They have received detailed information
in the AGM invitation, under the relevant agenda item.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our plan to convert
AIXTRON AG into an SE structure is motivated by the increasingly international
nature of our business activities. We believe </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">that the SE is a widely appreciated modern company
structure best suited for a worldwide active company residing in Europe.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_150948_7748"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">3.
Results of Operations</font></b></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<h3 style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.1. Development of
Revenues</font></b></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
the first three months of 2010, AIXTRON recorded revenues of EUR&nbsp;154.5m,
an increase of EUR&nbsp;108.3m, or 234%, compared to EUR&nbsp;46.2m in the same
period last year. This year on year growth is made more significant in
comparison, by the declining investment cycle and effects of the global
recession, seen in Q1/2009, which resulted then, in the lowest recorded revenue
quarter of 2009. Compared to the previous quarter, Q1/2010 revenues also
increased sequentially, by 31% from EUR&nbsp;117.9m in Q4/2009. In addition to
the absolute sequential quarter sales volume effect, the revenue increase in
Q1/2010 was also favorably influenced by the strengthening of the US Dollar
(plus 6%) during the first quarter of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
quarterly sequential and year on year increases in revenues were mainly due to
the increase from compound semiconductor deposition equipment revenues </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(Q1/2010:
EUR 141.5m; Q4/2009: EUR 107.5m; Q1/2009: EUR 41.9m)</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">. The equipment sold is
predominantly used by customers for the production of LEDs, which are primarily
used currently as backlighting devices in products such as TVs, monitors,
laptops, netbooks, tablet PCs and emerging lighting applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Revenues
from silicon semiconductor deposition production equipment, used by customers
to manufacture NAND Flash and DRAM memory devices and logic applications, have
been insignificant in all three described quarters Q1/2009, Q4/2009, and
Q1/2010 and continue to suffer from the hesitancy of customers to invest into
the technology nodes addressed by AIXTRON at this stage.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total
equipment sales generated 93% of total revenues in Q1/2010 (91% in Q4/2009 and
Q1/2009). The remaining revenues were generated by sales of spare parts and
service, which showed signs of increasing volume towards the end of the
quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">94%
of total revenues in Q1/2010 were generated by sales to customers in Asia and
were 26 percentage points higher than the 68% recorded in Q1/2009, when the
European revenue share was relatively high at 25%, specifically influenced by
the Plastic Logic order revenue recorded in that period. The remaining Q1/2010
revenues were generated in Europe (2%) and the USA (4%).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cost of
sales</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased year on year, by 204%, from EUR&nbsp;25.2m in Q1/2009 (</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Q4/2009:
EUR&nbsp;62.4m) </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">to EUR&nbsp;76.6m in Q1/2010, while cost of sales
relative to revenues, significantly improved to 50% from 55% in Q1/2009 (53% in
Q4/2009). This year on year improvement was mainly due to increasing volume,
offsetting the negative US Dollar effect. The 3 percentage point sequential
quarter improvement of cost of sales relative to revenues, mainly came from the
stronger average USD/EUR exchange rate and a more favorable product mix, in
addition to the above mentioned volume effect.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company&#146;s <b>gross profit</b> increased, in line with
revenue and cost of sales development, by 271% year on year and 40%
sequentially to EUR&nbsp;77.9m in Q1/2010 (Q1/2009: EUR&nbsp;21.0m; Q4/2009:
EUR&nbsp;55.5m), resulting in a higher <b>gross margin</b> of
50%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Operating
costs</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased year on year by 135% and by 45% quarter on quarter to EUR
31.5m (Q1/2009: EUR&nbsp;13.4m; Q4/2009: EUR&nbsp;21.8m). Operating costs
relative to revenues were 20% in Q1/2010, 2 percentage points higher than the
18% in Q4/2009, but 9 percentage points lower than in Q1/2009. This development
was influenced by the following factors:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Selling
expenses</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased year on year (to a lesser extent than
revenues), by 157% to EUR&nbsp;11.8m (Q1/2009: EUR&nbsp;4.6m), mainly against a
backdrop of higher volume related warranty expenses and sales commissions,
which vary by territory, partially offset by controlled discretionary expenses.
Selling costs relative to revenues decreased year on year by two percentage
points to 8%. In a quarter on quarter comparison, selling expenses (Q4/2009:
EUR&nbsp;9.1m) increased in line with volume and as a consequence of a
different geographical mix of sales. They remained stable at 8%, when related
to revenues.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
year on year and quarterly increase in<b> general and administration
expenses</b> by 61% and 42% to EUR&nbsp;7.4m in Q1/2010 (Q1/2009:
EUR&nbsp;4.6m; Q4/2009: EUR&nbsp;5.2m) was principally due to profit-related
variable administration expenses and investments in infrastructure. General and
administration expenses, relative to revenues, decreased from 10% in Q1/2009 to
5% in Q1/2010 (4% in Q4/2009).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Research
and development costs</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased by 21% year on year, from the EUR
8.9m recorded in Q1/2009 and increased 33% sequentially from the EUR 8.1m
recorded in Q4/2009, to EUR&nbsp;10.8m in Q1/2010, due to the increase in
development activities, including; additional personnel, material expenses and
depreciation. R&amp;D costs decreased in relative terms from 19% of revenues in
Q1/2009 to the same ratio of 7% in Q1/2010 and Q4/2009. However, AIXTRON&#146;s
R&amp;D investment activities are expected to remain strong in the years to
come, with the increased development focus on the R&amp;D center being built at
the Company&#146;s Herzogenrath/Aachen County premises. This investment
concentration supports the Company&#146;s determination to remain a major player in
markets judged by many to hold significant growth opportunities for many years
to come.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7<a name="PB_7_150948_7608"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
<b>other operating income and expenses</b> in
the first three months of 2010 resulted in an expense of EUR&nbsp;1.5m,
compared with EUR&nbsp;4.7m of income in Q1/2009. Included in the other
operating income recorded in Q1/2009 were the one-off gains made from the sale
of the Aachen office building of EUR 1.3m and </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a compensation
payment for a cancelled order of EUR 2.5m. A</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> currency expense of
EUR&nbsp;2.6m, largely from hedging contracts, was incurred</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> in
Q1/2010, but was </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">partially offset by EUR 1.1m of R&amp;D grants,
received during the period. This compares with a net expense of EUR 1.3m in
Q1/2009 due to </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">currency</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> effects from the USD/EUR
exchange rate movements. The net other operating income of EUR 0.6m in Q4/2009
mainly consists of R&amp;D grants, received during the quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
<b>operating result</b> significantly
increased by 511%, from EUR 7.6m in Q1/2009 to EUR 46.4m in Q1/2010 with a near
doubling of the EBIT margin to 30%. In a quarterly sequential comparison, the
operating result increased by 38% (or 1 percentage point), from EUR 33.7m (or
29% margin) in Q4/2009. This positive development was principally due to the
positive effects of the increase in revenue (including the strengthening of the
US Dollar, when comparing sequential quarters) and the factors described above.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Result
before taxes </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">increased by 480% from EUR 7.9m in Q1/2009 (Q4/2009:
EUR 34.4m) to EUR 45.8m in Q1/2010, with a finance expense of 1.0m in Q1/2010
arising from hedging contract expenses.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
recorded a <b>tax expense</b> of EUR 13.9m of the
profit before tax in the first three months of 2010, at a stable effective tax
rate of 30% (Q1/2009: EUR 2.4m or 30% of the profit before taxes; Q4/2009: EUR
10.0m or 29% tax rate).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
<b>net income</b> was 478% up year on year
from EUR 5.5m (12% of revenues) in Q1/2009, and 30% up quarter on quarter from
EUR 24.4m (21% of revenues) in Q4/2009 to reach EUR 31.8m (21% of revenues) in
Q1/2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.3. Development of
Orders</font></b></h3>

  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">%</font></b></p>

 <tr>
  <td width="38%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:38.0%;">

  <td width="5%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:5.5%;">

  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
with revenue development; <b>equipment order intake</b>
in Q1/2010 continued its progressively increasing quarterly trend. Q1/2010 was
the fourth sequential quarter of rising order intake, and at EUR 168.5m was 3%
up sequentially, and 440% up year on year (Q4/2009: EUR 163.3m; Q1/2009: EUR
31.2m). AIXTRON&#146;s own market intelligence continues to support the previously
expressed Executive Board Management opinion that the changes in the market
dynamics and environment are more likely to lead to a plateau of already high
demand rather than the two-quarter-peaks the industry has seen in the past. It
is too early to say how long the plateau will last.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
in previous quarters, almost the total value of Q1/2010 equipment orders (EUR
164.5m, 98%) came from compound semiconductor equipment customers (Q4/2009 and
Q1/2009: both 98%). The order intake for compound semiconductor equipment
increased by 438% in a year on year comparison, and by 3% sequentially.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
continuing positive market development is primarily driven by the increased
adoption of LED backlighting in TV and other display applications, representing
the &#145;Second LED Investment Cycle&#146;. However, included in the recent order intake
are a small number of orders linked to new lighting </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8<a name="PB_8_150948_8146"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='8',FILE='C:\JMS\C900569\10-8655-1\task4080273\8655-1-bc.htm',USER='c900569',CD='Apr 29 01:28 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">applications,
which may denote some early tentative positioning steps by customers towards an
emerging lighting market, which is seen by some as the &#145;Third Investment Cycle&#146;
for the LED industry. It is not yet clear how imminent or meaningful that
investment cycle is at this particular point in time, however, AIXTRON
Executive Board opinion is that current short term market activities and
developments could potentially positively influence the timing of an emergence
of a meaningful Solid State Lighting market in the mid term. The intention to
have developed the next generation AIXTRON system technology within the next
three years, reflects the Company&#146;s assumptions on the emergence of a
meaningful and sustainable Solid State Lighting market.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
proportion of orders received for silicon semiconductor equipment remained at
2% of total equipment order intake in Q1/2009, Q4/2009, and Q1/2010 reflecting
the very tentative investment sentiment in the memory and logic markets. In
absolute numbers, the order intake for silicon semiconductor equipment
increased from EUR 0.6m in Q1/2009 over EUR 3.6m in Q4/2009 to EUR 3.9m in
Q1/2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
total <b>equipment order backlog</b> of EUR 229.9m
at March&nbsp;31, 2010 was 128% higher than at the same point in time in 2009,
and 13% higher than the EUR 203.8m recorded as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 and
subsequently revalued to EUR 190.9m, reflecting the 2010 budget USD/EUR
exchange rate. 96% of the total Q1/2010 order backlog, i.e. EUR 220.2m,
consists of compound semiconductor orders (December&nbsp;31, 2009: 97%; March&nbsp;31,
2009: 93%). The remaining backlog figure of EUR 9.7m (4% of Q1/2010 backlog) is
made up of silicon system orders.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
a matter of internal policy, AIXTRON records only systems as order intake and
order backlog, if the Company has received a firm purchase order, an agreed
deposit, any specific shipment dependant documentation, and a system specific
customer-confirmed delivery date.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">4. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Financial Position</font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;"> and
Net Assets</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company recorded no <b>bank borrowings</b> as of March&nbsp;31, 2010
and December&nbsp;31, 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
<b>equity ratio</b> decreased to 64% as of March&nbsp;31,&nbsp;2010,
from 72% as of December&nbsp;31,&nbsp;2009, principally due to higher work in
progress and a consequently higher balance sheet total.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The AIXTRON Group&#146;s <b>capital
expenditures</b> of the first quarter of 2010 amounted to EUR 4.0m
(Q4/2009: EUR 3.2m; Q1/2009: EUR 2.9m), the large majority of which was related
to purchases of technical equipment (including testing and laboratory
equipment).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cash and
cash equivalents </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(including cash deposits with a maturity of more than
three months, most of which is held in Euros), increased by </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">23% to
EUR 371.6m (E</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">UR 250.6m + EUR 121.0m cash deposits) as of March&nbsp;31,&nbsp;2010
compared to </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR 301.2m (EUR 211.2m + EUR 90.0m cash deposits) </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">as of December&nbsp;31,
2009. Included in the period-end cash positions of the year 2009 and at
quarter-end Q1/2010 are the net proceeds from the October&nbsp;2009 capital
increase of EUR 157.6m.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The value of <b>property, plant and equipment</b> increased to
EUR&nbsp;39.4m as per March&nbsp;31, 2010 (</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR
37.8m as of December&nbsp;31, 2009), principally due to an increase in
laboratory equipment (with depreciation partly offsetting investments in
technical equipment) and the initial investments into the building of the new
R&amp;D center.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The increase in the value of <b>goodwill </b>from
</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR 58.3m as per December&nbsp;31, 2009 t</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">o
EUR</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> 61.0m as
per March&nbsp;31, 2010 resulted purely from currency translation adjustments.
There were no additions or impairments in the first three months of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The value of <b>other intangible assets</b>
decreased </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">from EUR 7.8m as per December&nbsp;31, 2009 to</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> EUR 7.5m as per March&nbsp;31,
2010 principally due to depreciation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Inventories</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">, including raw
materials, work in progress and finished goods, increased by only 14%, despite
the higher order and manufacturing
volume, from EUR 89.6m as of December&nbsp;31,
2009 to EUR 102.5m as of March&nbsp;31, 2010, all of which relates to
increased work in progress.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Trade receivables</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> also significantly
increased from </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR 49.3m</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 to EUR 73.8m as of March&nbsp;31, 2010 directly due to the increased business volume.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10<a name="PB_10_151609_4141"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.
Opportunities and Risks</font></b></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON believes that the following market trends and <b>opportunities</b> of the relevant end user markets could have a
positive effect on future business:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Short
Term</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Continuing
investment into capacity expansion for the production of LED backlighting for
LCD screens (netbooks, tablets, laptops, monitors, TVs).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Further increased
adoption of LEDs in automotive (e.g. interior lighting, headlights and rear
lights) or other applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased
adoption of LEDs for exterior, public street and professional lighting.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Mid Term</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased
adoption of LEDs for consumer and residential general lighting applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased
emergence of high volume Silicon Carbide (SiC) production applications and
emerging hybrid automotive and photovoltaic transistor applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased
emergence and further development of plastic electronics / flexible organic TFT
backplanes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development of
next generation NAND, DRAM and PRAM memory applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased
development activity for specialized compound solar cell applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Long Term</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Further progress
in research activities leading to technologies for OLED lighting and displays
as well as organic material large area deposition.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Progress in the
convergence development of new complex semiconductor material applications as
substituting materials in the silicon semiconductor industry.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development of
new applications using Carbon Nanostructures (Carbon Nanotubes or Carbon
Nanowires).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON is exposed to a series of <b>risks</b>
which are described in detail in the &#147;Risk Report&#148; of the Annual Report 2009
and in the section &#147;Risk Factors&#148; in AIXTRON&#146;s 2009 20-F-Report, which has been
filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission on March&nbsp;10, 2010.
Copies of the Company&#146;s most recent Annual Report and Form&nbsp;20-F are
available on the Company&#146;s website at www.aixtron.com (sections &#147;Investors/Reports&#148;
and &#147;Investors/US-Listing&#148;), as well as on the SEC&#146;s website at www.sec.gov.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">International Rectifier Corporation (I.R.), of El
Segundo, California, USA filed a complaint on September&nbsp;8, 2008 in the
U.S. District Court for the Central District of California against seven of
I.R.&#146;s former employees, including I.R.&#146;s founder and former CEO Alex Lidow, as
well as five companies, including AIXTRON AG. I.R.&#146;s complaint alleged that
I.R.&#146;s seven former employees misappropriated, divulged to a business named
Efficient Power conversion Corporation (EPCC) and illegally used trade secrets
of I.R. relating to Gallium Nitride Technology (GaN). I.R. also alleged that
some of the companies, including AIXTRON aided the seven main defendants by
providing additional information relevant to the technology at issue. In February&nbsp;2009,
the U.S. District Court dismissed the two U.S. federal claims in the case
against the defendants and declined to exercise its discretionary jurisdiction
over the remaining claims, which all arose under California law. Having had its
lawsuit dismissed in the U.S. District Court, I.R. re-filed essentially the
same lawsuit in California state court in March&nbsp;2009 based on the
California state claims alone, and alleged five causes of action against
AIXTRON. After multiple rounds of motions to dismiss, I.R. dropped some of its
claims against the defendants, and the California court dismissed additional
claims. Two of I.R.&#146;s claims, one for alleged misappropriation of trade secrets
and one for alleged breach of contract, remain in the case against AIXTRON AG.
The lawsuit seeks USD 61m in damages jointly and severally against all of the
defendants, plus exemplary damages and attorneys&#146; fees and legal costs against
AIXTRON AG, and punitive damages against other defendants. AIXTRON AG fully
rejects the allegations contained in I.R.&#146;s California lawsuit and is
vigorously defending itself against the two remaining claims raised in I.R.&#146;s
California action against AIXTRON AG. Furthermore, AIXTRON AG filed an action
in the Aachen Landgericht in Germany (case no. 41 O 121/08) for a negative
declaratory judgment against I.R. with the aim of establishing in Germany, and
in the U.S., that all allegations and claims that I.R. raised against AIXTRON
AG are unfounded (the &#147;German action&#148;). In the German action, I.R.
counterclaimed for injunctive relief and damages. On April&nbsp;7, 2009, the
Aachen Landgericht issued a judgment in favor of AIXTRON AG and against I.R. on
all of AIXTRON AG&#146;s claims and all of I.R.&#146;s counterclaims in the German
action. The time for I.R. to appeal from the judgment in the German action has
expired, and the judgment in favor </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11<a name="PB_11_151609_8627"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">of AIXTRON AG and against I.R. in the German action is
now final and res judicata. AIXTRON AG reserves the right to seek recovery from
I.R. of any and all costs and damages that might result from I.R.&#146;s unjustified
allegations and the proceedings brought by I.R. against AIXTRON AG.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:ideograph-numeric ideograph-other;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first three months of 2010, AIXTRON
Management was not aware of any further significant additions or changes in the
risks as described in the 2009 Annual Report/20-F-Report referred to above.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12<a name="PB_12_151609_7906"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">6. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Outlook</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It
is already clear that 2010 will be another growth year for us. We began the
year with a very solid order backlog as a foundation for that growth, which has
been further strengthened by the business recorded during the first three
months of the year. In Q1/2010, we have already made excellent progress towards
the objective of making the necessary adjustments to the operations functions
and support infrastructure to ensure record manufacturing output levels during
2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
expect that virtually all of the Q1/2010 period end backlog of EUR 229.9m will
be converted into revenues before the end of the year 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Reflecting the current healthy climate, the Executive
Board has raised the 2010 full year guidance to a range of EUR 650-700m revenue
with an EBIT margin of circa 30%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Due to multiple emerging market applications for LED products, we </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">also remain optimistic on the evident medium to
long term trend</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">. Both, market volume and the penetration rate of LEDs
as backlighting units in products such as netbooks, tablets, laptops, monitors
and TVs, are expected to continue to grow over the next 3-5 years, and the
adoption of LEDs for general lighting applications is expected to increase.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
will continue to closely watch the USD/EUR exchange rate and the potential
effects on the Company&#146;s revenues and profitability and will employ appropriate
financial instruments to mitigate potential risk.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
the coming nine months of the year, we plan to continue to invest in laboratory
equipment and to complete the roll out of the group-wide SAP Enterprise
Software System. Investments in the building of the new R&amp;D center at our
premises in Herzogenrath/Aachen County are expected to reach EUR 15m by the end
of the year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
continue to believe that our Company has sufficient funds or instruments in
place to ensure that the foreseeable needs of the business can be met.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
at March&nbsp;31, 2010, we had no binding agreements for participation
financing, company acquisitions or transfers of parts of the Company.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13<a name="PB_13_151609_3736"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Additional Disclosures</font></b></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">1. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Accounting Policies</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
consolidated interim financial report of AIXTRON AG has been prepared in
accordance with International Financial Reporting Standards (IFRS) applicable
for Interim Financial Reporting, IAS 34.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
accounting policies adopted in this interim financial report are consistent
with those followed in the preparation of the Group&#146;s annual financial
statements for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
consolidated interim financial statements of AIXTRON AG include the following
operating subsidiaries (collectively referred to as &#147;AIXTRON&#148;, &#147;the AIXTRON
Group&#148;, or &#147;the Company&#148;): AIXTRON,&nbsp;Inc., Sunnyvale (USA); AIXTRON Ltd.,
Cambridge (United Kingdom); AIXTRON AB, Lund (Sweden); AIXTRON Korea Co. Ltd.,
Seoul (South Korea); AIXTRON KK, Tokyo (Japan); and AIXTRON Taiwan Co. Ltd.,
Hsinchu (Taiwan). There were no changes in the consolidated group of companies
in comparison with December&nbsp;31, 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">2. </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Segment Reporting</font></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following
segment information has been prepared in accordance with IFRS 8 &#147;Operating
Segments&#148;. As AIXTRON has only one operating segment, the information provided
relates only to geographical data.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company markets and sells its products in Asia,
Europe, and the United States, mainly through its direct sales organization and
cooperation partners.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In presenting information on the basis of geographical
segments, segment revenue is based on the geographical location of customers.
Segment assets are based on the geographical location of the assets.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

representing the right to receive AIXTRON AG common shares or AIXTRON AG
American Depositary Shares (ADS). The status of these options developed as
follows:</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">4.

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The total number of full time equivalent employees
rose from 621 on March&nbsp;31, 2009 to 731 persons on March&nbsp;31, 2010.</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">5. Management</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
compared to December&nbsp;31, 2009, there were no changes to the composition of
the Company&#146;s Executive and Supervisory Boards as of March&nbsp;31, 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">6. Related Party Transactions</font></b></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON
did not conclude or carry out any material transactions with related parties.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">7.
Post-Balance Sheet Date Events</font></b></h2>

<h2 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">There
were no known business events with a potentially significant effect on AIXTRON&#146;s
results of operation, financial position or net assets after March&nbsp;31,
2010.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">19<a name="PB_19_151609_5250"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:-.2pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:0pt;">Responsibility Statement</font></b></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To the best of our
knowledge, and in accordance with the applicable reporting principles for
interim financial reporting, the interim consolidated financial statements for
the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2010 give a true and fair view of the
assets, liabilities, financial position and profit or loss of the group, and
the interim management report of the group includes a fair review of the
development and performance of the business and the position of the group,
together with a description of the principal </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">opportunities
and risks associated with the expected development of the group for the
remaining months of the financial year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Herzogenrath, April&nbsp;2010</font></p>
